# this container build continues from rhel.Dockerfile and rhel.Dockefile.extract.assets.sh
# assumes you have created asset-*.tar.gz files for all arches, but you'll only unpack the one for your arch

# https://access.redhat.com/containers/?tab=tags#/registry.access.redhat.com/ubi8-minimal
FROM sha256:332744c1854d8e87f41dc67bf3d7e1c08d7a6b1322b5b5bd0b126bf8282ca1f8
RUN mv -f /etc/yum.repos.d/ubi.repo /tmp || :
ADD tls-ca-bundle.pem /tmp/tls-ca-bundle.pem
ADD atomic-reactor-repos/* /etc/yum.repos.d/
COPY asset-*.tar.gz /tmp/assets/
RUN microdnf -y install tar gzip shadow-utils && \
    adduser appuser && \
    tar xzf /tmp/assets/asset-configbump-$(uname -m).tar.gz -C / && \
    rm -fr /tmp/assets/ && \
    chmod 755 /usr/local/bin/configbump && \
    microdnf -y remove tar gzip shadow-utils && \
    microdnf -y update || true && \
    microdnf -y clean all && rm -rf /var/cache/yum && \
    echo "Installed Packages" && rpm -qa | sort -V && echo "End Of Installed Packages"
USER appuser
ENTRYPOINT ["configbump"]

# append Brew metadata here
ENV SUMMARY="Red Hat CodeReady Workspaces configbump container" \
DESCRIPTION="Red Hat CodeReady Workspaces configbump container" \

# this container build continues from rhel.Dockerfile and rhel.Dockefile.extract.assets.sh
# assumes you have created asset-*.tar.gz files for all arches, but you'll only unpack the one for your arch

# https://access.redhat.com/containers/?tab=tags#/registry.access.redhat.com/ubi8-minimal
FROM sha256:1264d9863dfd9bedef87ff83d69e194ccdbf2b636d78284d2379cdd3e0d54eff
RUN mv -f /etc/yum.repos.d/ubi.repo /tmp || :
ADD tls-ca-bundle.pem /tmp/tls-ca-bundle.pem
ADD atomic-reactor-repos/* /etc/yum.repos.d/
COPY asset-*.tar.gz /tmp/assets/
RUN microdnf -y install tar gzip shadow-utils && \
    adduser appuser && \
    tar xzf /tmp/assets/asset-configbump-$(uname -m).tar.gz -C / && \
    rm -fr /tmp/assets/ && \
    chmod 755 /usr/local/bin/configbump && \
    microdnf -y remove tar gzip shadow-utils && \
    microdnf -y update || true && \
    microdnf -y clean all && rm -rf /var/cache/yum && \
    echo "Installed Packages" && rpm -qa | sort -V && echo "End Of Installed Packages"
USER appuser
ENTRYPOINT ["configbump"]

# append Brew metadata here
ENV SUMMARY="Red Hat CodeReady Workspaces configbump container" \
DESCRIPTION="Red Hat CodeReady Workspaces configbump container" \
PRODNAME="codeready-workspaces" \
COMPNAME="configbump-rhel8"

name="$PRODNAME/$COMPNAME" \

# this container build continues from rhel.Dockerfile and rhel.Dockefile.extract.assets.sh
# assumes you have created asset-*.tar.gz files for all arches, but you'll only unpack the one for your arch

# https://access.redhat.com/containers/?tab=tags#/registry.access.redhat.com/ubi8-minimal
FROM sha256:88b7feca21692b223bbfc4e12eb4de0f39aab52f114b767e159dcc1d6a14cc1e
RUN mv -f /etc/yum.repos.d/ubi.repo /tmp || :
ADD tls-ca-bundle.pem /tmp/tls-ca-bundle.pem
ADD atomic-reactor-repos/* /etc/yum.repos.d/
COPY asset-*.tar.gz /tmp/assets/
RUN microdnf -y install tar gzip shadow-utils && \
    adduser appuser && \
    tar xzf /tmp/assets/asset-configbump-$(uname -m).tar.gz -C / && \
    rm -fr /tmp/assets/ && \
    chmod 755 /usr/local/bin/configbump && \
    microdnf -y remove tar gzip shadow-utils && \
    microdnf -y update || true && \
    microdnf -y clean all && rm -rf /var/cache/yum && \
    echo "Installed Packages" && rpm -qa | sort -V && echo "End Of Installed Packages"
USER appuser
ENTRYPOINT ["configbump"]

# append Brew metadata here
ENV SUMMARY="Red Hat CodeReady Workspaces configbump container" \
DESCRIPTION="Red Hat CodeReady Workspaces configbump container" \
PRODNAME="codeready-workspaces" \
COMPNAME="configbump-rhel8"

io.openshift.expose-services="" \
usage=""

# this container build continues from rhel.Dockerfile and rhel.Dockefile.extract.assets.sh
# assumes you have created asset-*.tar.gz files for all arches, but you'll only unpack the one for your arch

# https://access.redhat.com/containers/?tab=tags#/registry.access.redhat.com/ubi8-minimal
FROM ubi8-minimal:8.3-298.1618432845
COPY asset-*.tar.gz /tmp/assets/
RUN microdnf -y install tar gzip shadow-utils && \
    adduser appuser && \
    tar xzf /tmp/assets/asset-configbump-$(uname -m).tar.gz -C / && \
    rm -fr /tmp/assets/ && \
    chmod 755 /usr/local/bin/configbump && \
    microdnf -y remove tar gzip shadow-utils && \
    microdnf -y update || true && \
    microdnf -y clean all && rm -rf /var/cache/yum && \
    echo "Installed Packages" && rpm -qa | sort -V && echo "End Of Installed Packages"
USER appuser
ENTRYPOINT ["configbump"]

# this container build continues from rhel.Dockerfile and rhel.Dockefile.extract.assets.sh
# assumes you have created asset-*.tar.gz files for all arches, but you'll only unpack the one for your arch

# https://access.redhat.com/containers/?tab=tags#/registry.access.redhat.com/ubi8-minimal
FROM ubi8-minimal:8.3-298.1618432845
COPY asset-*.tar.gz /tmp/assets/
RUN microdnf -y install tar gzip shadow-utils && \
    adduser appuser && \
    tar xzf /tmp/assets/asset-configbump-$(uname -m).tar.gz -C / && \
    rm -fr /tmp/assets/ && \
    chmod 755 /usr/local/bin/configbump && \
    microdnf -y remove tar gzip shadow-utils && \
    microdnf -y update || true && \
    microdnf -y clean all && rm -rf /var/cache/yum && \
    echo "Installed Packages" && rpm -qa | sort -V && echo "End Of Installed Packages"
USER appuser
ENTRYPOINT ["configbump"]

# this container build continues from rhel.Dockerfile and rhel.Dockefile.extract.assets.sh
# assumes you have created asset-*.tar.gz files for all arches, but you'll only unpack the one for your arch

# https://access.redhat.com/containers/?tab=tags#/registry.access.redhat.com/ubi8-minimal
FROM ubi8-minimal:8.3-298.1618432845
COPY asset-*.tar.gz /tmp/assets/
RUN microdnf -y install tar gzip shadow-utils && \
    adduser appuser && \
    tar xzf /tmp/assets/asset-configbump-$(uname -m).tar.gz -C / && \
    rm -fr /tmp/assets/ && \
    chmod 755 /usr/local/bin/configbump && \
    microdnf -y remove tar gzip shadow-utils && \
    microdnf -y update || true && \
    microdnf -y clean all && rm -rf /var/cache/yum && \
    echo "Installed Packages" && rpm -qa | sort -V && echo "End Of Installed Packages"
USER appuser
ENTRYPOINT ["configbump"]
